<script type="text/javascript">
    

    amznJQ.onReady('jQuery', function() {
        var attachEntityAlert = function() {
            var entityAlertContainer = jQuery('#entity-alert');
            var entityAlertSavingMsg = entityAlertContainer.find('.saving-action');

            entityAlertContainer.find(".entity-alert-body.subscription-action").each(function() {
                var currentMessage = jQuery(this);
                var subscriptionAction = currentMessage.find(".subscription-action");

                var url, eventToBind;
                if (subscriptionAction.attr('href')) {
                    url = subscriptionAction.attr("href");
                    eventToBind = 'click';
                } else if (subscriptionAction.attr('action')) {
                    var url = subscriptionAction.attr("action");
                    eventToBind = 'submit';
                } else {
                    return;
                }

                var ajaxHandlerUrl = "/gp/entity-alert/external/entity-alert-subscription-ajax-handler.html";

                var urlParts = url.split('?');
                var urlParts2 = urlParts[0].split("/ref=");
                var params = "";

                if (urlParts2.length > 1) {
                    ajaxHandlerUrl += "/ref=" + urlParts2[1];
                }
                if (urlParts.length > 1) {
                    params= urlParts[1];
                }

                var currentState = currentMessage.attr('class').replace('entity-alert-body', '');

                subscriptionAction.bind(eventToBind, function() {
                    jQuery.ajax({
                        url: ajaxHandlerUrl,
                        async: true,
                        type: "POST",
                        dataType: "json",
                        cache: false,
                        data: params,
                        beforeSend: function() {
                            // Also explicitly alter the CSS because the style for detail page widget is all inlined
                            currentMessage.removeClass("show").css("display", "none");
                            entityAlertSavingMsg.addClass("show").css("display", "block");
                        },
                        success: function(data, textStatus) {
                            if (data.redirect) {
                                window.location.href = data.redirect;
                            } else {
                                var newState = data.subscriptionState;
                                // Also explicitly alter the CSS because the style for detail page widget is all inlined
                                entityAlertSavingMsg.removeClass("show").css("display", "none");
                                entityAlertContainer.find("." + newState).addClass("show").css("display", "block");
                            }
                        },
                        error: function(data, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                            var newState;

                            if (currentMessage.hasClass('not-subscribed') || currentMessage.hasClass('not-signed-in')) {
                                newState = 'error-subscribe';
                            } else if (currentMessage.hasClass('subscribed')) {
                                newState = 'error-unsubscribe';
                            } else {
                                newState = 'generic-error';
                            }

                            // Also explicitly alter the CSS because the style for detail page widget is all inlined
                            entityAlertSavingMsg.removeClass("show").css("display", "none");
                            entityAlertContainer.find("." + newState).addClass("show").css("display", "block");
                        }
                    });
                    return false;
                });
            });
        };
        attachEntityAlert();
    });

</script>

<h2 style="margin:0">Videos</h2>
<div id="artist-page-airy-video-player"  style="width: 300px; height: 241px;"></div>
<div id="artistCentralVideos_controls" style="display:none">
    <div style="width:100%; height:26px; font-size:10px; line-height:12px; text-align:center; margin-top:3px">
        <div style="color:gray; font-size:10px; font-family:arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">Provided by the artist or their representative</div>
        <div id="artistCentralVideos_caption"></div>
    </div>

    <div style="display:none" id="artistCentralVideos_video_title_0">One Night Only- Anniversary Edition DVD Trailer</div>
<script type="text/javascript">
    function ArtistPageAiryPlayer() {
        this.mediaContexts = [{'mediaSourceInfo':'https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/I/C1xj0NhROqS.mp4',}];
        this.instance = Airy.embed({"streamingUrls":"https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/I/C1xj0NhROqS.mp4","contentTitle":"One Night Only- Anniversary Edition DVD Trailer","parentId":"artist-page-airy-video-player","foresterMetadataParams":{"requestId":"052P6AYQAQQV3G4E05P1","marketplaceId":"ATVPDKIKX0DER","session":"180-1753812-2724733"},"swfUrl":"http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/vap/video/airy2/prod/2.0.989.0/flash/AiryBasicRenderer._V328693797_.swf"});
        jQuery( '#artistCentralVideos_controls' ).show();
    };

    ArtistPageAiryPlayer.prototype.playVideo = function(oldIndex, newIndex) {
        if (oldIndex != newIndex) {
            var video = this.mediaContexts[newIndex];
            this.instance.loadMedia({mediaSourceInfo : video.mediaSourceInfo
            });
            artistCentralVideos_setCaption(newIndex);
            this.instance.play();
        }
    };

    function artistCentralVideos_setCaption(index) {
        var element = jQuery('#artistCentralVideos_caption');
        if (element.size() != 1) return;
        var text = jQuery('#artistCentralVideos_video_title_' + index).text();
        if (text.length == 0) {
            element.text('');
            return;
        }
        element.text('...');
        var maxHeight = element.attr('offsetHeight') * 2 - 1;
        element.text(text);
        if (element.attr('offsetHeight') > maxHeight) {
            var numChars = 1;
            element.text(text.substr(0, numChars) + '...');
            while ((numChars < text.length) && (element.attr('offsetHeight') <= maxHeight)) {
                ++numChars;
                element.text(text.substr(0, numChars) + '...');
            }
            --numChars;
            while ((numChars > 0) && (text.charAt(numChars - 1) == ' ')) {
                --numChars;
            }
            element.text(text.substr(0, numChars) + '...');
        }
    };

    var artistPageAiryPlayer;
    amznJQ.onReady('Airy', function() {
        artistPageAiryPlayer = new ArtistPageAiryPlayer();
        artistCentralVideos_setCaption(0);
    });
</script>

    var artistCentralShuffler_gallery = {
        displayedImageIndex: 0,
        displayedPageIndex: 0,

        select: function(index) {
            if (1) {
                artistCentralGalleryOnSelect( artistCentralShuffler_gallery.displayedImageIndex, index );

                artistCentralShuffler_gallery.displayedImageIndex = index;
            }
        },
        displayNextPage: function() {
            artistCentralShuffler_gallery.changePage(artistCentralShuffler_gallery.displayedPageIndex + 1);
            return false;
        },
        displayPrevPage: function() {
            artistCentralShuffler_gallery.changePage(artistCentralShuffler_gallery.displayedPageIndex - 1);
            return false;
        },
        changePage: function(index) {
            jQuery( "#artistCentralShuffler_galleryPage" + artistCentralShuffler_gallery.displayedPageIndex ).hide();
            jQuery( "#artistCentralShuffler_galleryPage" + index ).show();
            artistCentralShuffler_gallery.displayedPageIndex = index;

  <script type="text/javascript">
<!--
tgSearch = new Object();

(function($) {
tgSearch.strings = new Object();
tgSearch.asins = new Object();
tgSearch.taggedItems = new Array();
tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN = new Object();
tgSearch.searchFieldClicked = 0;
tgSearch.searchResults = new Array();
tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN = new Object();
tgSearch.currentPage = 0;
tgSearch.currentSearch = 0;
tgSearch.resultsLoaded = 0;
tgSearch.resultsPage = 0;
tgSearch.resultsPageSize = 100;
tgSearch.searchValue = '';
tgSearch.searchAlias = '';
tgSearch.searchAliasName = '';
tgSearch.lastElement = -1;
tgSearch.lastPage = -1;
tgSearch.alternateKeywords = new Array();
tgSearch.title = '';
tgSearch.hasInited = 0;
tgSearch.numberTagged = -1;

tgSearch.itemAlreadyTagged = new Object();
tgSearch.recentASINs = new Array();
                                                                                                                                                             
tgSearch.lastChance = new Object();
                                                                                                                                                             
tgSearch.TIMEOUT = 10000;

/*
 Success handler for removing a tag.  Removes item from the tagged item queue and re-inserts it
 into the search results at the correct position, and decrements tag count
*/
removeTagResults = function(t, tagCountString){
  if(t.status != 'error'){
    t.action = 'removed';
    if(t.searchNumber == tgSearch.currentSearch){
      s = tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[t.ASIN.asin];
      s.status = 'show';
    }
  }else{
    var undoDiv = jQuery("#undo_" + t.ASIN.asin);
    undoDiv.html('<div class="tgSearchError tiny">' + tgSearch.strings.tagErrorMessage + '</div>' + displayUndoButton());
    return;
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  var sibid = 'searchItemButton' + t.ASIN.asin;
  var sib = jQuery("#" + sibid);
                                                                                                                                                             
  //deleting the tagged item will reinforce queue ordering if it's re-tagged
  delete tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[t.ASIN.asin];
  removeTaggedItem(t);                                                                                                                                                           
  delete t;
                                                                                                                                                             
  if(sib != null){
    sib.html(displayAddTagButton(a));
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  if(tagCountString != ''){
    updateTagCount(tagCountString);
  }
  
  displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage);
}

/*
 Make an asynchronous service call to remove your tag from an item
*/
submitRemoveTag = function(t){
  var options = {
    url : "/gp/tagging/addproducts/remove.html/ref=" + tgSearch.ref + "_rmv",
    data: {asin : t.ASIN.asin, tgTag : tgSearch.tag, count : tgSearch.numberTagged, sessionID : tgSearch.sessionID},
    error : function() { errorRemoveFunction(tgSearch.tag, t.ASIN.asin,t); },
    success : successRemoveFunction,
    cache : false,
    timeout : tgSearch.TIMEOUT,
    dataType: "json",
    type: "POST",
    async: true
  };

  jQuery.ajax(options);  
}

/*
  Success handler for removal
*/
successRemoveFunction = function(data,textStatus) {
  thisTaggedItem = getTaggedItemByASIN(data['asin']);
  thisTaggedItem.status = data['status'];
  thisTaggedItem.enabled = 'false';
  tgSearch.numberTagged = data['numberTagged'];
  removeTagResults(thisTaggedItem,data['tagCountString']);
}

/*
 Error handler for removal
*/
errorRemoveFunction = function(tag,asin,t){
  if(tgSearch.lastChance[asin]){
    var undoDiv = jQuery("#undo_" + asin);
    undoDiv.html('<div class="tgSearchError tiny">' + tgSearch.strings.tagErrorMessage + '</div>' + displayUndoButton(t));
    tgSearch.lastChance[asin] = undefined;
  }else{
    tgSearch.lastChance[asin] = 1;
    submitRemoveTag(t);
  }
}


/*
 Display an undo button, unless you tagged the item in a previous session
*/
displayUndoButton = function(t){
  if(t.action == 'ptagged'){
    var undoButton = '<span class="tgSearchAlreadyTagged">' + tgSearch.strings.alreadyTagged + '</span>';
  }else{
    var undoButton = '<span class="tgSearchUndo">' +
      '<span class="tgSearchTaggedText">' + tgSearch.strings.taggedMessage + '</span>' +
      '(<a href="javascript: void(0)" class="tgSearchUndoLink" onClick="removeTag(' +
              String.fromCharCode(0x27) + t.ASIN.asin + String.fromCharCode(0x27) +
              ');return false;">' + tgSearch.strings.undoMessage + '</a>' +
      '</span>)';
  }
  return undoButton;
}

/*
 Display a single tagged item stripe, with the appropriate action/message/icon.
*/
displayTaggedItem = function(t){
  var taggedItemDisplay = '<td style="padding: 4px;" id="undo_' + t.ASIN.asin + '" width="90" align="center">';
    if(t.status == 'waiting'){
      taggedItemDisplay += displayWaitingIcon();
    }else if(t.status == 'adderr'){
      taggedItemDisplay += '<div class="tgSearchError tiny">' + tgSearch.strings.tagErrorMessage +'</div>' + displayAddTagButton(t.ASIN);
    }else{
      taggedItemDisplay += displayUndoButton(t);
    }
  taggedItemDisplay += '</td>' +
  displayASIN(t.ASIN, 'tiny', t.status == 'waiting');
  return taggedItemDisplay;
}

/*
 Helper for addTag, actually sets up and makes the asynchronous call to tag an item
*/
submitAddTag = function(t){
  var options = {
    url : "/gp/tagging/addproducts/add.html/ref=" + tgSearch.ref + "_rmv",
    data: {asin : t.ASIN.asin, tgTag : tgSearch.tag, count : tgSearch.numberTagged, sessionID : tgSearch.sessionID},
    error : function() { errorAddFunction(t.ASIN.asin,t); },
    success : successAddFunction,
    cache : false,
    timeout : tgSearch.TIMEOUT,
    dataType: "json",
    type: "POST",
    async: true
  };
  jQuery.ajax(options);
}

/*
 Success handler for adding a tag
*/
successAddFunction = function(data,textStatus) {
  thisTaggedItem = getTaggedItemByASIN(data['asin']);
  thisTaggedItem.status = data['status'];
  thisTaggedItem.enabled = data['enabled'];
  tgSearch.numberTagged = data['numberTagged'];
  addTagResults(thisTaggedItem, data['tagCountString']);
}

/*
 Error handler for adding a tag
*/
errorAddFunction = function(asin,t){
  if(tgSearch.lastChance[asin]){
    t.status = 'adderr';
    updateTaggedItem(t);
    tgSearch.lastChance[asin] = undefined;
  }else{
    tgSearch.lastChance[asin] = 1;
    submitAddTag(t);
  }
}


/*
 Display a search result, with the correct action button
*/
displaySearchResult = function(a, status){
  var t = null;
                                                                                                                                                             
  if(tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[a.asin] != null){
    t = tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[a.asin];
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  if(tgSearch.itemAlreadyTagged[a.asin]){
    if(t != null){
      t.action = 'ptagged';
    }
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  var button;
  if(tgSearch.itemAlreadyTagged[a.asin]){
    button = '<span class="tgSearchAlreadyTagged">' + tgSearch.strings.alreadyTagged +'</span>';
  }else if(status == 'waiting'){
    button = displayWaitingIcon();
  }else if(t != null && t.action != 'removed'){
    button = '<span class="tgSearchTagged">' + tgSearch.strings.taggedMessage + '</span>';
  }else{
    button = displayAddTagButton(a);
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  var searchResultDisplay = '<td id="searchItemButton' + a.asin + '" class="tiny" style="color: #9d0000; padding: 4px;" align="center">' +
    button +
    '</td>' +
    displayASIN(a, 'tiny');
  return searchResultDisplay;
}

/*
 For the case when there are no search results and no suggestions, show that to the user
 and suggest they try again
*/
displayNullSearchResults = function(){
  jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").scrollTop = 0;
                                                                                                                                                             
  var searchResultsDisplay = tgSearch.strings.searchNoResultsMessage;
  if(tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length > 0){
    searchResultsDisplay += displayAlternateKeywords();
  }
  jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").html(searchResultsDisplay);
  jQuery("#tgSearchNavigationDiv").html('');
}

/*
 Displays a single ASIN row in search results
*/
displayASIN = function(a,fontClass,translucent){
  if(fontClass == null){
    fontClass = 'small';
  }
  if(translucent == undefined){
    translucent = 0;
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  //display an ASIN
  var linkedTitle = '<a class="tgSearchItemTitle" href="' + a.url + '">' + a.title + '</a>';
  var thumbDisplay;
  if(a.thumb != null){
    thumbDisplay = a.thumb;
  }else{
    thumbDisplay = '&nbsp;';
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  var bylineDisplay = '';
  if(a.byline != ''){
    bylineDisplay = tgSearch.strings.byLine + ' ' + a.byline;
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  var bindingDisplay = '';
  if(a.binding != ''){
    bindingDisplay = ' <span class="tgSearchBinding">(' + a.binding + ')</span>';
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  var asinDisplay = '<td ';
  if(translucent){
    asinDisplay += 'class="tgSearchTranslucent" ';
  }
  asinDisplay +=  'style="padding:4px;" width="44">' + thumbDisplay + '</td>' +
    '<td class="' + fontClass ;
  if(translucent){
    asinDisplay += ' tgSearchTranslucent';
  }
  asinDisplay += '" style="padding: 4px;">' +
    linkedTitle +
    '<br />' +
    bylineDisplay +
    bindingDisplay +
    '</td>';
  return asinDisplay;
}


/*
 If there are search suggestions, show them to the user and allow a 1-click re-search
*/
displayAlternateKeywords = function(){
  if(tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length == 0){
    return;
  }
  var alternateString = '<div class="tgSearchAlternate">' + tgSearch.strings.alternateMessage;
                                                                                                                                                             
  for(i=0; i<tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length; i++){
    keyword = tgSearch.alternateKeywords[i];
    alternateString += ' <a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="doAlternateSearch(' +
        String.fromCharCode(0x27) + keyword + String.fromCharCode(0x27) +
        ');return false;">' + keyword + '</a>';
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  alternateString += tgSearch.strings.alternateEndMessage + '</div>';
  return alternateString;
}

/*
 Returns a waiting icon
*/
displayWaitingIcon = function(){
  var waitingIcon = tgSearch.images.waiting;
  return waitingIcon;
}
                                                                                                                                                             
/*
 Returns the "Tag This" button
*/
displayAddTagButton = function(a){
  //show add tag button
  var addTagButton = '<a href="#" onClick="addTag(this,' + String.fromCharCode(0x27) +
      a.asin + String.fromCharCode(0x27) +
      ');return false;" title="' + tgSearch.strings.tagThisMessage + '">' + tgSearch.images.tag +'</a>';
  return addTagButton;
}

/*
 Insert the given item in the tagged items panel (at the beginning)
*/
addTaggedItem = function(item){
  var itemTable = jQuery('#taggedItemsTable');
  item.jqObj = jQuery('<tr id="tgTagItem_' + item.ASIN.asin + '" asin="' + item.ASIN.asin + '">' + displayTaggedItem(item) + '</tr>').prependTo(itemTable);
  item.jqObj.after(displayDivider());
}

/*
 Update the given tagged item, refreshing its status
*/
updateTaggedItem = function(item){
  if(typeof item == 'undefined' || typeof item.jqObj == 'undefined'){
    return;
  }
  item.jqObj.html(displayTaggedItem(item));
}

/*
 Remove the given tagged item from the tagged items panel
*/
removeTaggedItem = function(item){
  if(typeof item == 'undefined' || typeof item.jqObj == 'undefined'){
    return;
  }
  if(item.jqObj.next().attr('class') == 'tiDivider'){
    item.jqObj.next().remove();
  }
  item.jqObj.remove();
}

displayDivider = function(){
  return '<tr class="tiDivider"><td colspan="4" style="border-top: 1px solid #eee;">' + tgSearch.images.pixel + '</td></tr>';
}

/*
 Renders a next button
*/
displayNextTeaser = function(){
  var nextTeaser = '<td align="center" id="tgSearchNextTeaserButton">' +
    '<a href="#" onClick="displaySearchResults(' +
    (tgSearch.currentPage + 1) +
    ',1);return false;">' + tgSearch.images.next + '</a>' +
    '</td>' +
    '<td colspan="2" id="tgSearchNextTeaserText">' +
    '<span class="tgSearchNextTeaser">' + tgSearch.strings.nextTeaserMessage +'</span>' +
    '</td>';
  return nextTeaser;
}

/*
 Show a loading icon, given a location to show it in.
*/
showLoading = function(location){
  if(location != null){
    var msg = tgSearch.strings.loadingMessage;
    location.html(msg + ' ' + tgSearch.images.loading);
  }
}

/*
 Renders and displays search results to the user
*/
displaySearchResults = function(page, reset){
  tgSearch.currentPage = page;
  //reset the search div's scroll for IE's sake
  if(reset){
    jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").scrollTop = 0;
  }
  if(tgSearch.resultsLoaded - (page * tgSearch.searchPageSize) <= 50 && tgSearch.lastElement == -1){
    startSearch(0);
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  if((page * tgSearch.searchPageSize) > tgSearch.resultsLoaded && tgSearch.lastElement == -1){
    var msg = tgSearch.strings.loadingMessage;
    jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").html(msg + ' ' + tgSearch.images.loading);
    return;
  }
  jQuery("#tgSearchTitle").html(tgSearch.title);
  var pageStart = (page - 1) * tgSearch.searchPageSize;
  var pageEnd = (page * tgSearch.searchPageSize) - 1;
                                                                                                                                                             
  //iterate through results and call displaySearchResult
  var resultsShown = 0;
  var searchResultsDisplay = '<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">';
  for(var i=pageStart; i<pageEnd; i++){
    if(tgSearch.searchResults[i] == null){
      break;
    }
    if(tgSearch.searchResults[i].ASIN.asin != null){
      var item = tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[tgSearch.searchResults[i].ASIN.asin];
      if(item.status != 'show'){
        continue;
      }
      resultsShown++;
      searchResultsDisplay += '<tr id="tgSearchItem_' + tgSearch.searchResults[i].ASIN.asin + '">' +
        displaySearchResult(tgSearch.searchResults[i].ASIN, tgSearch.searchResults[i].status) +
        '</tr>';
    }
  }
  if(!resultsShown && (tgSearch.lastElement == -1  || tgSearch.lastElement >= (tgSearch.searchPageSize * tgSearch.currentPage))){
    searchResultsDisplay += '<tr>' +
    displayNextTeaser() +
    '</tr>';
  }
  searchResultsDisplay += '</table>';
   
  jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").html(searchResultsDisplay);
  displaySearchNavigation();
}

/*
 This function decides whether there is a next page to show, and if we can go
 to a previous page, and renders buttons below the search pane to let the user
 perform the available actions
*/
displaySearchNavigation = function(){
  var searchNavigationDisplay;
  if(tgSearch.currentPage >= 1){
    var hasNextPage;
// If there is no last element defined yet, or we're not on the last page, we can go further
    if(tgSearch.lastElement == -1 || tgSearch.lastElement >= (tgSearch.searchPageSize*tgSearch.currentPage)){
      hasNextPage = 1;
    }else{
      hasNextPage = 0;
      tgSearch.lastPage = tgSearch.currentPage;
    }
                                                                                                                                                             
    var itemInfoText;
    itemInfoText = '<b class="tiny">' + tgSearch.strings.infoMessage + ' ' + tgSearch.currentPage;
    if(tgSearch.lastPage != -1){
       itemInfoText += ' of ' + tgSearch.lastPage;
    }
    itemInfoText += '</b>';
                                                                                                                                                             
    searchNavigationDisplay =
      '<table class="tgSearchNavTable" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">' +
      '<tr><td width="50%">&nbsp;</td>';
                                                                                                                                                             
    if(tgSearch.currentPage > 1){
      searchNavigationDisplay += '<td align="right">' +
        '<a href="#" onClick="displaySearchResults(' +
        (tgSearch.currentPage - 1) +
        ', 1);return false;" title="' + tgSearch.strings.previousMessage + '">' + tgSearch.images.previous + '</a>' +
        '</td>';
    }
                                                                                                                                                             
    if(itemInfoText != null){
      searchNavigationDisplay += '<td align="center" class="tgSearchNavInfo">' +
        itemInfoText +
        '</td>';
    }
    if(hasNextPage){
     searchNavigationDisplay += '<td align="left">' +
       '<a href="#" onClick="displaySearchResults(' +
       (tgSearch.currentPage + 1) +
       ',1);return false;" title="' + tgSearch.strings.nextMessage + '">' + tgSearch.images.next + '</a>' +
       '</td>';
    }
                                                                                                                                                             
    searchNavigationDisplay += '<td width="50%">&nbsp;</td></tr>' +
      '</table>';
  }else{
    searchNavigationDisplay = '';
  }
  if(searchNavigationDisplay != null){
    jQuery("#tgSearchNavigationDiv").html(searchNavigationDisplay);
  }
}

/*
 If the search fails more than once, display an error
*/
showSearchError = function(){
  jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").html(tgSearch.strings.searchError);
}

/*
 Constructor for an ASIN, given the thumbnail image, title, url, byline, binding, and image URL.
*/
ASIN = function(jsonData) {
  this.asin = jsonData['asin'];
  this.thumb = jsonData['image'];
  this.title = jsonData['title'];
  this.url = jsonData['url'];
  this.byline = jsonData['byline'];
  this.binding = jsonData['binding'];
  this.imageURL = jsonData['imageURL'];

  jQuery.preloadImage(this.imageURL);
                                                                                                                                                             
  //add a reference to this object to make it discoverable
  tgSearch.asins[this.asin] = this;
}

/*
 Construct a TaggedItem, giving it an asin, an action (tagged/undone/previously tagged), a current status,
 and a search number
*/
TaggedItem = function(a,action,status,searchNumber){
  this.ASIN = a;
  this.action = action;
  this.status = status;
  this.searchNumber = searchNumber;
                                                                                                                                                             
  tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[a.asin] = this;
}
                                                                                                                                                             
/*
 Construct a SearchResult, given an ASIN, an action, and the current status.
*/
SearchResult = function(a,action,status){
  this.ASIN = a;
  this.action = action;
  this.status = status;
                                                                                                                                                             
  tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[a.asin] = this;
}
                                                                                                                                                             
/*
 Retrieve a tagged item using its ASIN
*/
getTaggedItemByASIN = function(asin){
  var t = tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[asin];
  return t;
}

/*
 Kick off an asynchronous search, using the value in the search box.
 If this is not a brand-new search, then just fetch more results for the current search term.
*/
startSearch = function(newSearch){
  var pageNumber = 1;
  if(newSearch){
    var alias = jQuery("#tgSearchAlias").attr('value');
    var sValue = jQuery("#tgSearchValue").attr('value');
    if(sValue.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'') == ''){
      return;
    }
    if(alias == tgSearch.searchAlias && sValue == tgSearch.searchValue){
      showSearchResults();
      return;
    }
    tgSearch.searchAlias = alias;
    tgSearch.searchValue = sValue.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');
    tgSearch.currentPage = 1;
    tgSearch.currentSearch++;
    tgSearch.searchResults = new Array();
    tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN = new Object();
    tgSearch.resultsLoaded = 0;
    tgSearch.resultsPage = 1;
    tgSearch.searchAliasName = jQuery("#tgSearchAlias option:selected").text();
    tgSearch.lastElement = -1;
    tgSearch.lastPage = -1;
    tgSearch.alternateKeywords = new Array();
    jQuery("#tgSearchTitle").html('');
    jQuery("#tgSearchNavigationDiv").html('');
  } else {
    pageNumber = tgSearch.resultsPage - 1;
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  //assemble the search URL
  var options = {
    url : "/gp/tagging/addproducts/search.html/ref=" + tgSearch.ref + "_src",
    data: {value : tgSearch.searchValue, page : pageNumber, pageSize : tgSearch.resultsPageSize, index : tgSearch.searchAlias,
      alias : tgSearch.searchAliasName, queryNo : tgSearch.currentSearch, source : tgSearch.source},
    error : searchErrorHandler,
    success : searchSuccessFunction,
    cache : false,
    timeout : tgSearch.TIMEOUT,
    dataType: "json",
    type: "POST",
    async: true
  };
  
  if (newSearch) {
    tgSearch.resultsPage++;
                                                                                                                                                             
    showSearchResults();
                                                                                                                                                             
    showLoading(newSearch?jQuery('#tgSearchDiv'):null);
  }
  jQuery.ajax(options);
}

searchSuccessFunction = function(data,textStatus) {
  if (data['queryNo'] == tgSearch.currentSearch) {
 
    tgSearchData = new Object;
    if (data['nextPage']) {
      tgSearchData.nextPage = data['nextPage'];
    }
    if (data['prevPage']) {
      tgSearchData.prevPage = data['prevPage'];
    }
    tgSearchData.startingItem = data['startingItem'];
    tgSearchData.endingItem = data['endingItem'];
    tgSearchData.itemsReturned = data['asinList'].length;
    tgSearchData.itemsFound = data['itemsFound']
    tgSearchData.title = data['resultsTitle'];
    if (data['correctedKeywords']) {
      tgSearchData.title += '<div class="tgSearchCorrected">' + data['correctedKeywords'] + '</div>';
    }
    if (data['lastItem']) {
      tgSearch.lastElement = data['lastItem'];
    }
    tgSearch.alternateKeywords = data['keywordList'];
    searchResults(data['asinList'],tgSearchData);
  }
}

/*
 If the search fails, try again
*/
searchErrorHandler = function(){
  startSearch(0);
}

/*
 Success handler for retrieving search results
*/
searchResults = function(results,searchData){
  var title = searchData.title;
                                                                                                                                                             
  tgSearch.resultsLoaded += searchData.itemsReturned;
                                                                                                                                                             
  for(i=0; i<results.length; i++){
    var tmpASIN = new ASIN(results[i]);
    if(tmpASIN.asin != null){
      tgSearch.searchResults.push(new SearchResult(tmpASIN, 'add',tgSearch.itemAlreadyTagged[tmpASIN.asin]?'ptagged':'show'));
    }
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
// If we got results, check to see if there might be alternate searches.
  if( searchData.itemsReturned > 0){
    if(tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length > 0){
      title += displayAlternateKeywords();
    }
    tgSearch.title = title;
    displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage);
  }else{
// If we didn't get results, try to show search suggestions - if there aren't any, display no results
    if(tgSearch.resultsLoaded > 0){
      tgSearch.lastElement = tgSearch.resultsLoaded;
      if(tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length > 0){
        title += displayAlternateKeywords();
      }
      tgSearch.title = title;
      displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage);
    }else{
      displayNullSearchResults();
    }
  }
}

/*
 Called on 1-click re-search from alternate keywords.  Simply resets the contents of the search
 box to the new search term and performs a new search.
*/
doAlternateSearch = function(keyword){
  jQuery("#tgSearchValue").attr("value",keyword);
  startSearch(1);
}

/*
 Make an asynchronous call to tag the desired asin.  The button clicked must be
 passed in so we can change it to a waiting icon.  This function just sets up
 the waiting and item statuses, and calls a helper to make the actual call.
*/
addTag = function(button,asin){
  //Find the ASIN
 a = tgSearch.asins[asin];
 s = tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[asin];
 s.status = 'tagged';
 displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage,0);
                                                                                                                                                             
  if(getTaggedItemByASIN(asin) != null){
    t = getTaggedItemByASIN(asin);
    t.action = 'add';
    t.status = 'waiting';
  }else{
    t = new TaggedItem(a,'add','waiting',tgSearch.currentSearch);
    tgSearch.taggedItems.push(t);
  }
 
  addTaggedItem(t); 
  
  submitAddTag(t);
}

/*
 Success handler for addTag.  Updates the "you've tagged x products count by
 incrementing, as relying on the TaggingService to return that count in a transactional
 way turns out to be a bad idea.
*/
addTagResults = function(t,tagCountString){
  if(t.status != 'error'){
    t.action = 'added';
    tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[t.ASIN.asin].status = 'tagged';
    displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage,0);
  }else{
    t.status = 'adderr';
    updateTaggedItem(t);
    return;
  }
                                                                                                                                                             
  if(tagCountString != ''){
    updateTagCount(tagCountString);
  }

  updateTaggedItem(t);
  jQuery("#taggedItemsDiv").scrollTop = 0;
}

/*
 Update your tag count with the given string
*/
updateTagCount = function(tagCountString){
  jQuery("#tgSearchTagCount").html(tagCountString);
}
                                                                                                                                                             

/*
 Remove your tag from an item
*/
removeTag = function(asin){
  t = tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[asin];
                                                                                                                                                             
  t.status = 'waiting';
  t.action = 'remove';
  updateTaggedItem(t);
  
  submitRemoveTag(t);
}

/*
 Reveals the search results pane
*/
showSearchResults = function(){
  var divsToShow = ['tgSearchTitle','tgQueueTitle','tgSearchResultsContainer','tgQueueContainer'];
  for(var div=0;div<divsToShow.length;div++){
    jQuery("#" + divsToShow[div]).removeClass('tgSearchHidden');
  }
}

/*
 Hides the search results pane
*/
hideSearchResults = function(){
  var divsToShow = ['tgSearchTitle','tgQueueTitle','tgSearchResultsContainer','tgQueueContainer'];
                                                                                                                                                             
  for(var div=0;div<divsToShow.length;div++){
    jQuery("#" + divsToShow[div]).addClass('tgSearchHidden');
  }
}

/*
 Clears the search input box
*/
clearSearchField = function(){
  if(tgSearch.searchFieldClicked){
    return;
  }
  jQuery("#tgSearchValue").select().attr("class","").addClass("tgSearchBlack");
  tgSearch.searchFieldClicked = 1;
}
})(jQuery);
//-->
</script>
